The described changes\\n25: // are not applied directly, but contain an approximation of the final\\n26: // result that will be completed during apply by resolving any values that\\n27: // cannot be predicted.\\n28: //\\n29: // A plan must always be accompanied by the configuration it was built from,\\n30: // since the plan does not itself include all of the information required to\\n31: // make the changes indicated.\\n32: type Plan struct {\\n33: \\t// Mode is the mode under which this plan was created.\\n34: \\t//\\n35: \\t// This is only recorded to allow for UI differences when presenting plans\\n36: \\t// to the end-user, and so it must not be used to influence apply-time\\n37: \\t// behavior. New behavior\\n42: \\t// should not be added based on this flag, and changing the flag should be\\n43: \\t// checked carefully against existing destroy behaviors.\\n44: \\tUIMode Mode\\n45: \\n46: \\t// VariableValues, VariableMarks, and ApplyTimeVariables together describe\\n47: \\t// how Terraform should decide the input variable values for the apply\\n48: \\t// phase if this plan is to be applied.\\n49: \\t//\\n50: \\t// VariableValues and VariableMarks describe persisted (non-ephemeral)\\n51: \\t// values that were set as part of the planning options and are to be\\n52: \\t// re-used during the apply phase. VariableValues can potentially contain\\n53: \\t// unknown values for a speculative plan, but the variable values must\\n54: \\t// all be known for a plan that will subsequently be applied.\\n55: \\t//\\n56: \\t// ApplyTimeVariables retains the names of any ephemeral variables that were\\n57: \\t// set (non-null) during the planning phase and must therefore be\\n58: \\t// re-supplied by the caller (potentially with different values) during\\n59: \\t// the apply phase. If not then the plan was created successfully but found\\n95: \\t// no material differences between desired and prior state, and so\\n96: \\t// applying this plan would achieve nothing.\\n97: \\tApplyable bool\\n98: \\n99: \\t// Errored is true if the Changes information is incomplete because\\n100: \\t// the planning operation failed. An errored plan cannot be applied,\\n101: \\t// but can be cautiously inspected for debugging purposes.\\n102: \\tErrored bool\\n103: \\n104: \\t// Checks captures a snapshot of the (probably-incomplete) check results\\n105: \\t// at the end of the planning process.\\n106: \\t//\\n107: \\t// If this plan is applyable (that is, if the planning process completed\\n108: \\t// without errors) then the set of checks here should be complete even\\n109: \\t// though some of them will likely have StatusUnknown where the check\\n110: \\t// condition depends on values we won't know until the apply step.\\n111: \\tChecks *states.CheckResults\\n112: \\n113: \\t// RelevantAttributes is a set of resource instance addresses and\\n114: \\t// attributes that are either directly affected by proposed changes or may\\n115: \\t// have indirectly contributed to them via references in expressions.\\n116: \\t//\\n117: \\t// This is the result of a heuristic and is intended only as a hint to\\n118: \\t// the UI layer in case it wants to emphasize or de-emphasize certain\\n119: \\t// resources. Don't use this to drive any non-cosmetic behavior, especially\\n120: \\t// including anything that would be subject to compatibility constraints.\\n121: \\tRelevantAttributes []globalref.ResourceAttr\\n122: \\n123: \\t// PrevRunState and PriorState both describe the situation that the plan\\n124: \\t// was derived from:\\n125: \\t//\\n126: \\t// PrevRunState is a representation of the outcome of the previous\\n127: \\t// Terraform operation, without any updates from the remote system but\\n128: \\t// potentially including some changes that resulted from state upgrade\\n129: \\t// actions.\\n130: \\t//\\n131: \\t// PriorState is a representation of the current state of remote objects,\\n132: \\t// which will differ from PrevRunState if the \\\"refresh\\\" step returned\\n133: \\t// different data, which might reflect drift.\\n134: \\t//\\n135: \\t// PriorState is the main snapshot we use for actions during apply.\\n136: \\t// PrevRunState is only here so that we can diff PriorState against it in\\n137: \\t// order to report to the user any out-of-band changes we've detected.\\n138: \\tPrevRunState *states.State\\n139: \\tPriorState   *states.State\\n140: \\n141: \\t// ExternalReferences are references that are being made to resources within\\n142: \\t// the plan from external sources.\\n143: \\t//\\n144: \\t// This is never recorded outside of Terraform. It is not written into the\\n145: \\t// binary plan file, and it is not written into the JSON structured outputs.\\n146: \\t// The testing framework never writes the plans out but holds everything in\\n147: \\t// memory as it executes, so there is no need to add any kind of\\n148: \\t// serialization for this field. This does mean that you shouldn't rely on\\n149: \\t// this field existing unless you have just generated the plan.\\n150: \\tExternalReferences []*addrs.Reference\\n151: \\n152: \\t// Overrides contains the set of overrides that were applied while making\\n153: \\t// this plan. We need to provide the same set of overrides when applying\\n154: \\t// the plan so we preserve them here. distinct address appears only once.\\n172: func (p *Plan) ProviderAddrs() []addrs.AbsProviderConfig {\\n173: \\tif p == nil || p.Changes == nil {\\n174: \\t\\treturn nil\\n175: \\t}\\n176: \\n177: m[key]\\n195: \\t}\\n196: \\n197: \\treturn ret\\n198: }\\n199: \\n200: // Backend represents the backend-related configuration and other data as it\\n201: // existed when a plan was created.\\n202: Although the values for these variables can\\n62: \\t// change between plan and apply, their \\\"nullness\\\" may not.\\n63: \\tVariableValues     map[string]DynamicValue\\n64: \\tVariableMarks      map[string][]cty.PathValueMarks\\n65: \\tApplyTimeVariables collections.Set[string]\\n66: \\n67: \\tChanges           *ChangesSrc\\n68: \\tDriftedResources  []*ResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n69: \\tDeferredResources []*DeferredResourceInstanceChangeSrc\\n70: \\tTargetAddrs       []addrs.Targetable\\n71: \\tForceReplaceAddrs []addrs.AbsResourceInstance\\n72: \\tBackend           Backend\\n73: \\n74: \\t// Complete is true if Terraform considers this to be a \\\"complete\\\" plan,\\n75: \\t// which is to say that it includes a planned action (even if no-op)\\n76: \\t// for every resource instance object that was mentioned across both\\n77: \\t// the desired state and prior state.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// If Complete is false then the plan might still be applyable (check\\n80: \\t// [Plan.Applyable]) but after applying it the operator should be reminded\\n81: \\t// to plan and apply again to hopefully make more progress towards\\n82: \\t// convergence.\\n83: \\t//\\n84: \\t// For an incomplete plan, other fields of this type may give more context\\n85: \\t// about why the plan is incomplete, which a UI layer could present to\\n86: \\t// the user as part of a warning that the plan is incomplete.\\n87: \\tComplete bool\\n88: \\n89: \\t// Applyable is true if both Terraform was able to create a plan\\n90: \\t// successfully and if the plan calls for making some sort of meaningful\\n91: \\t// change.\\n92: \\t//\\n93: \\t// If [Plan.Errored] is also set then that means the plan is non-applyable\\n94: \\t// due to an error. Copyright (c) HashiCorp, Inc.\n// SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.\n// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchangesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\t// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\tvar output strings.Builder\n\n\t// Define the order of actions to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Process each action type in order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges, ok := changesByAction[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s resources:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceType := rc.Addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := rc.Addr.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Build the full resource address\n\t\t\tvar addr string\n\t\t\tif rc.Addr.Module.IsRoot() {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s\", resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"module.%s.%s.%s\", strings.Join(rc.Addr.Module.Module().Names(), \".\"), resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\toutput.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tcounts := countChanges(changesByAction)\n\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy\\n\",\n\t\tcounts[plans.Create]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]+counts[plans.CreateThenForget],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Update],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Delete]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete],\n\t))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete, plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// actionSymbol returns a short symbol for an action type\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"-/+\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"+/-\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"+/.\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a map of action counts\nfunc countChanges(changesByAction (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.\n// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchangesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\t// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\tvar output strings.Builder\n\n\t// Define the order of actions to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Process each action type in order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges, ok := changesByAction[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s resources:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceType := rc.Addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := rc.Addr.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Build the full resource address\n\t\t\tvar addr string\n\t\t\tif rc.Addr.Module.IsRoot() {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s\", resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"module.%s.%s.%s\", strings.Join(rc.Addr.Module.Module().Names(), \".\"), resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\toutput.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tcounts := countChanges(changesByAction)\n\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy\\n\",\n\t\tcounts[plans.Create]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]+counts[plans.CreateThenForget],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Update],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Delete]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete],\n\t))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete, plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// actionSymbol returns a short symbol for an action type\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"-/+\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"+/-\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"<=\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \".\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"+/.\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"?\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// countChanges returns a map of action counts\nfunc countChanges(changesByAction map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc) map[plans.Action]int {\n\tcounts := make(map[plans.Action]int)\n\tfor action, changes := range changesByAction {\n\t\tcounts[action] = (\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\t\"strings\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter produces a condensed, summary-style diff output\n// for terraform plan, showing only resource-level changes without\n// attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a compact summary of changes in the plan, grouped by action type.\n// It displays one line per resource change showing the action and resource address.\nfunc (f *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\t// Group changes by action type\n\tchangesByAction := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\n\t// Iterate through all resource changes, filtering out deposed objects\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed keys (only show current objects)\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tchangesByAction[rc.Action] = append(changesByAction[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\tvar output strings.Builder\n\n\t// Define the order of actions to display\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t}\n\n\t// Process each action type in order\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tchanges, ok := changesByAction[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(changes) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(changes, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn changes[i].Addr.String() < changes[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action header\n\t\tactionLabel := actionLabel(action)\n\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s resources:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\t// Write each resource change\n\t\tfor _, rc := range changes {\n\t\t\tresourceType := rc.Addr.Resource.Resource.Type\n\t\t\tresourceName := rc.Addr.Resource.Name\n\n\t\t\t// Build the full resource address\n\t\t\tvar addr string\n\t\t\tif rc.Addr.Module.IsRoot() {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"%s.%s\", resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\taddr = fmt.Sprintf(\"module.%s.%s.%s\", strings.Join(rc.Addr.Module.Module().Names(), \".\"), resourceType, resourceName)\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  [%s] %s\\n\", actionSymbol(action), addr))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\toutput.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tcounts := countChanges(changesByAction)\n\toutput.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Plan: %d to add, %d to change, %d to destroy\\n\",\n\t\tcounts[plans.Create]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete]+counts[plans.CreateThenForget],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Update],\n\t\tcounts[plans.Delete]+counts[plans.DeleteThenCreate]+counts[plans.CreateThenDelete],\n\t))\n\n\treturn output.String()\n}\n\n// actionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action type\nfunc actionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create, plans.CreateThenForget, plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete, plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.NoOp:\n\t\treturn \"No-op\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// actionSymbol returns a short symbol for an action type\nfunc actionSymbol(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"+\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"-\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"~\"\n\tcase
